Squabbling over Hot Water Leads to Fight

Detective Wang Licheng Stabbed

Yang Fuxing Halal Noodle Shop, owned by Yang Si, a native of Yangzhou, has been located at No. 55 Anna Jin Road, behind the Slaughterhouse Company in the French Concession. Yesterday morning around 9:00, Yang's wife, Zhang, went to the boiling water stove downstairs at the Longqing Teahouse at No. 69 nearby to get hot water. A quarrel arose over whether the water was boiling or not, and Zhang slapped a Guan surnamed waiter. The waiter retaliated by pushing Zhang into the road, causing her to fall and become covered in mud. Both sides went to the Songshan Road Police Station, where the police chief ordered each to pay a fine of one yuan as a warning. After returning home, Zhang complained to her husband, Yang Si, who was furious. He immediately gathered dozens of colleagues from the Henan gang and went to the boiling water stove to cause trouble. At that time, the owner of the Longqing Teahouse, Wang Dekui, heard the news and rushed to mediate. He invited the owner of the boiling water stove, Liu Changde, to have tea upstairs. Wang explained the misunderstanding and instructed Liu to bear the full amount of the fines imposed by the police on both sides. He also ordered Liu to pour tea and apologize to Yang to settle the matter. However, Yang firmly refused, insisting that Liu buy firecrackers and send Zhang home. Liu refused, and before they could come to an agreement, Yang ordered a violent attack. At that time, police detective Wang Licheng happened to be at the teahouse on business and was stabbed in the jaw with a sharp axe. They also tried to snatch the pistol that Wang was carrying. After being injured, Wang immediately reported to the police station, which dispatched detectives and arrested three people, including Yang Si, for investigation.

Lion Brand Beef Extract Price Increase Imminent

The various medicines managed by the German merchant Huada Pharmacy in this city are all products that meet the needs of the medical community in our country and have long been well-known. Among them, Lion Brand Beef Extract is the world's most famous tonic medicine, which mainly treats all kinds of deficiencies and has remarkable effects. It is especially popular among the Chinese people. The pharmacy has suffered heavy losses since the gold standard and silver devaluation crisis last year and the sharp increase in year-end tariffs. It has no choice but to slightly increase prices to maintain its operations. It is reported that it has been decided that from February 20th, the wholesale price of this beef extract will increase by 3 yuan from the original price, and the retail price will be 1 yuan per bottle and 20 yuan per dozen. The prices of other products will generally increase by 20%. However, Lion Brand Chicken Extract is still within the preferential period and will not increase in price accordingly. Those who are accustomed to taking the pharmacy's beef extract should purchase and store it before the 20th.

Letter

To the Editor: After reading the news item in your newspaper of the 13th of this month, "Jiang Youzhi's Letter to the French Concession," it is inconsistent with the facts. On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month, I received a phone call from my friend Fan Songji, saying that Dong Kang had repeatedly discussed the settlement of Jiang Youzhi's lawsuit and had drafted a concrete plan. I was asked to go and discuss it. I asked Mr. Fan whether it was correct that the other party was capricious. Mr. Fan replied that the other party had written evidence to prove it. I went to Mr. Fan's residence. Mr. Fan showed me the other party's written settlement conditions, which were signed and sealed by Wang Kanghou, the representative of the Jiang family. Only then did Yu believe it. Mr. Fan called again at about 7:00 p.m., saying that he had arranged to complete the deal at the New World Hotel and asked me to go to the appointment immediately. I went to the room of my friend Yan Zegao because I had a party talking at home. (249) I rested temporarily. I met Mr. Fan and said that the other party had opened room number 239. At that time, in addition to Yan Zegao, there were Hang Jun, Shi Jun, Xu Jun Chihen, Ping Jun Jinya, Zhan Jifeng, Yan Yinwu, and two lawyers and Mrs. Yan Zegao and Mrs. Zhan. It was not until midnight that Qiu Jun Zijia came again. Hang Jun and others did not go for my business, but for other negotiations. I have never been to the other party's room. Only Mr. Fan and others negotiated back and forth. It is reported that in room number 239, there were the other party himself, Wang Kanghou, and the secretary Cai, and two female guests whom Mr. Fan and others did not know. All the conditions were negotiated at that time, but because the other party requested cash and there was no way to raise it at midnight, and the parents had to be present, it was not established. The next day, the court opened the trial, and Attorney Wang also stated this in his statement, which can be verified in the record. The original manuscript suddenly claimed that he was coerced and chased, and a large number of unrelated men and women surrounded him. I really don't know what it is based on. It is ridiculous to deceive oneself and deceive others. All the gentlemen present are well-known people in society. It is not difficult to ask them about the truth. It is useless to listen to such slander and only lose their personality. I hereby submit the facts and hope that you will investigate and correct them to clarify the facts and correct the audience. Yu Don respectfully to the Shen Bao office.

Educational News

Headlines

Asian Education Conference

Our Country's Huang Qiming and Gao Jianfu Attend

Most of the Discussion Focuses on Indian Education Issues

丨Religious Boundaries Too Strict丨

丨India Lacks Secondary Education丨

(Guangzhou Correspondent) The Asian Education Conference was held in Benares, India, from December 26th to 30th last year. The representatives from our country were Huang Qiming, the principal of Guangzhou Peizheng Middle School, and Gao Jianfu, a famous Lingnan painter. Mr. Gao stayed in India to engage in art exhibitions at the invitation of local organizations. Mr. Huang has now returned to the country and returned to the province. The reporter believes that the Asian Education Conference is also related to our country. The people of our country want to know what the situation is. He specially visited Mr. Huang to inquire about everything. According to him, the Asian Education Conference was initiated by the World Education Association. The previous World Education Conference was held in Geneva. At the conference, at the request of the Indian representatives, the decision to hold this conference was made. This conference was held in Benares, India. Representatives from all Asian countries participated, but they were all overseas Chinese in the local area. There were three representatives specially sent by the country. The representatives from our country were Mr. Yu and Gao Jianfu. During the conference, from December 26th to 20th, for five consecutive days, the conference was attended by thousands of people. In addition to the representatives appointed by various countries, the rest were all educational figures from all parts of India. The discussion items were divided into women's education, civilian education, and secondary education groups. Mr. Yu was appointed as the chairman of the secondary education discussion group. In summary, this conference has very little relationship with our country, and Japan has absolutely none. It can be called the All-India Education Conference. Mr. Yu gave a detailed report on the status of secondary education in our country at the conference, and advised India to pay attention to secondary education. The Indians listened to this and were quite convinced by Mr. Yu's words. As for the status of education in India, it only has a deformed development. It only pays attention to higher education and does not pay attention to civilian education. Secondary education is even more lacking. Brothers have visited the International University founded by the poet Tagore. Although its scale is small, its facilities are quite complete. It has students of all races, and there are also two people from our country. Benares University has even more complete facilities and a very large scale. It is said that at the beginning of the establishment, it cost more than 10,000 yuan, all of which was automatically donated by the Indians. They pay so much attention to higher education, but it is a pity that they ignore secondary civilian education and do not know how to promote it. In recent years, the academic community has also been quite developed. For example, the Benares Literature Award and the Science Award have both been won by Indians. The Indians are most proud of this. It is not surprising that the Eastern spiritual civilization won the Literature Award, but it is enough for the Indian academic community to show a different color by winning the Science Award. Mr. Yu has traveled to various places and found that the squalor of the Indian countryside is worse than that of our country. The gap between the rich and poor classes among the people is too great. This may be due to the lack of secondary education. The strict religious boundaries are also a major reason for the slow evolution of the Indian nation. The boundaries between Hinduism and Islam are very strict. The followers of the two religions often clash. Therefore, even if they are united and single-minded in seeking national affairs, even the great leaders are inevitably bound by religion. Therefore, if India wants to seek national glory, it will not succeed without breaking the concept of religion. The president of Benares University, Mr. Morihua, once published the proposal of the two religions working together, but after Mr. Mo shook hands with Muslims, he always washed his hands after returning home, which shows how deep the concept of religion is. There was no public banquet at this conference, which is rare in Western countries. The reason is that everyone is restricted by religious doctrine and cannot eat together. Now the Indians still show goodwill towards our overseas Chinese, and they are no longer as discriminatory as before, and they hope that the next conference will be held in our country.

Ministry of Education Declares the Significance of Phonetic Symbols

The Ministry of Education, based on Chen Yicheng's request for a declaration on the meaning of phonetic symbols, issued a directive stating: "The submitted document has been reviewed and understood. The original submission contains many doubts about phonetic symbols. Generally speaking, these doubts are nothing more than not knowing the proper characters, the complexity of adding phonetic notations alongside reading, and the unaesthetic shapes of the characters. It is important to understand that the creation of phonetic symbols is precisely for those who do not know how to read to learn to read. The Chinese writing system is complex and difficult to recognize, which is a major obstacle to the popularization of education. The phonetic symbols, including initials and finals, total only forty. These symbols are simple and easy to recognize, easy to spell, and easy to annotate beside the proper characters, allowing one to recognize characters by recognizing the phonetic symbols. All books, documents, official notices, etc., can then be read, proper characters can be recognized, and knowledge can be increased. The establishment of phonetic symbols is precisely to encourage those who do not know how to read to learn to read and write, not to abandon proper characters once phonetic symbols are introduced, and to never need to further recognize proper characters or read books. Since these phonetic symbols are designed to assist in recognizing proper characters, they should naturally be annotated beside the proper characters and should not be separated in any way. How can it be suspected of being like 'building a bed under a house'? As for the shapes, the simple shapes and ease of recognition are precisely the characteristics of phonetic symbols. The shapes of proper characters each have their own strengths and should not be compared in terms of superiority. In short, all the concerns in the original submission are misunderstandings. The reason for these concerns is that the person who submitted the document is someone who already knows how to read. For someone who already knows how to read to then learn phonetic symbols, it is natural to feel somewhat inconvenienced. However, the number of people in our country who know how to read only accounts for 20% of the total population. The remaining 80%, or more than 30 million people, are mostly illiterate and need to learn to read and write through phonetic symbols. Therefore, promoting phonetic symbols is good news for those who do not know how to read. The Ministry has therefore promulgated measures for promoting phonetic symbols in various provinces and cities and is immediately distributing small booklets for phonetic symbol instruction to urge active implementation nationwide. The person who submitted the document has done little research on the effectiveness and significance of promoting phonetic symbols, so this special clarification is hereby issued for your information."

Pay attention to the introduction of practical and specific methods and the examination of efficiency after supervision.

Sports

Japan Revises Women's Basketball Rules

Adopting American Rules

Because the Current Rules are Too Drastic

World News Agency, Tokyo: The Japan YWCA is holding its 25th anniversary celebration. The association's sports department took the opportunity to initiate the revision of women's basketball rules and contacted women's sports organizations and sports departments of women's schools across the country to work towards implementing the new rules. According to Ms. Kawanishi Hatsuko, an officer of the association's sports department, the women's basketball rules currently used in Japan are the same as those for men. This sport is too intense. From the perspective of women's physical strength and its educational value, it is difficult to obtain good results. The new rules are based on the American women's basketball rules, which differ greatly from the traditional men's basketball rules. The old rules divided the entire game into two halves, while the revised rules divide it into four quarters. The rest time is set at two minutes each. The court is also divided into three sections, and the activities of WhileQuarterCentret are limited within the collection degree. In addition, there are also important differences in the shortening of game time and the use of venues. It is believed that after the application of these new rules, basketball will be simplified and popularized in the women's sports world.

Social News

Foch's Diary of the European War by a French General

Translated by Gu Ang Ruo

September 4th, my detachment was assigned all the army supplies it was due, and thus separated from the Fourth Army to become independent, officially forming the Ninth Army. Later, it received reinforcements from the Eighteenth Infantry Division (Ninth Army Corps), which had been temporarily stationed in Lulles since August 20th…

The task of the Ninth Army (September 9th) was very clear. No matter the difficulties, the army must support the battle force on the front line, prevent the enemy from breaking through the defense line, and prevent them from crossing the line, until victory was certain. Therefore, I repeatedly encouraged the soldiers to fight to the death, and told them about the enemy's situation in the remaining sections of the front, so that they would know my firm belief in our final victory.

According to reports received by the Ninth Army Headquarters, the German army had not stopped marching since the start of the war. Their perseverance had been pushed to the extreme. Many units had long lost their officers and non-commissioned officers. The regiments were in a state of chaos, and the general officers had lost control.

"The enemy firmly believes that we can no longer resist. Our brave attack will definitely catch the enemy off guard.

"The importance of taking advantage of this opportunity is difficult to overstate. I only hope that each of you will muster the remaining courage to make one last strike. Our nation will not lack this final enemy force when it is in a critical moment of survival.

"The chaos in the enemy's ranks is a harbinger of our victory.

"If you can contain them in one go today, tomorrow we can drive them out of our country.

"Remember that victory belongs to those who persevere the longest. France's reputation and full strength are still uncertain. Work hard, and you can win.

"The reports from the entire front are very good…"

Most importantly, the right wing of the Forty-Second Division has strong support. The Eleventh Army Corps now seems to be deployed to assist the division in combat. Colonel Weigand directly ordered the Twenty-First Division in Linser at five o'clock.

At 5:15, the Forty-Second Division attacked the Conno Court flour mill from the Linsevero line (north of Gaolei).

The Eleventh Army Corps has been ordered to attack on its entire line to assist the right wing of the division in its advance.

The Twenty-First Division immediately attacked the ridge northwest of Ouwei.

As for myself, I gave a final encouragement to the soldiers, calling on them to put all their energy into this attack. So, on the evening of September 9th, we launched a major counterattack from west to east towards Fuerxiang Benoia and its key areas.

Our soldiers were truly exhausted, but now, with another attack, we showed our determination to win, and we calculated that when the Forty-Second Division launched a full-scale attack, we would indeed have a chance to prevail against the enemy, who had been exhausted after days of fierce attacks. Moreover, the enemy's initial victory allowed them to advance so quickly to the south, and their position was therefore quite unstable.

The areas around Fuerxiangnuo and along the roads were littered with dead and wounded, which proves that the enemy had indeed suffered heavy losses. A large number of prisoners were captured, and spoils of war were continuously delivered. The enemy's panicked retreat had already shown signs.

The Allied counter-offensive on September 9th was underway. On the 10th, the German army began to retreat. By the 11th, it had collapsed from retreat. Foch's Ninth Army's advance was unimpeded. On the 12th, it actually crossed the Mang River. On that day, Foch added this sentence to the order of the day, "The plan has not changed. Attacks are underway everywhere. Pursuits are underway everywhere."

The Battle of the Mang River was coming to an end. It was indeed a great victory. It was the credit of Commander-in-Chief Joffre. He began planning this great battle on August 24th and

Page 22

commanded the battle until the end. After we suffered setbacks on the border, he immediately realized that the battle was not going well, so he stopped fighting and prepared to wait until he had replenished the weaknesses that had been discovered, and then resume fighting with renewed vigor. He employed powerful tactics in Belgium, fully understood the enemy's goals, and without hesitation, he redeployed his troops. Because some officers had evidence of incompetence, he redistributed all the officers. He set up a diversion in the west and continued to retreat until the appropriate moment, he ordered his troops to stop retreating. After the army turned around, he cleverly combined offensive and defensive warfare, and then used planned movements to give the enemy a fatal blow.

From Woerke to Lulles, the entire army fully understood that France could not survive another defeat, so they fought with great unity and effort. Senior commanders and their staff competed with each other to carry out their tasks, and helped each other with the best spirit of friendship. Soldiers fought until they were exhausted and hoarse, fell on the battlefield, got up and fought again, and fought even more fiercely.

This war further proves that the spirit of the army in wartime is a reflection of the nation's deepest feelings. When these latent forces are well guided by a capable commander-in-chief, great historical achievements are established. This is the meaning of the Battle of the Mang River.

Paris, the heart of France, is now saved by the victory in which her direct protectors participated. Their military authorities sent them to the battlefield because the survival of the French capital was at stake.

The German plan failed, and the German prestige was completely swept away. The swift and fierce offensive, hoping to make France collapse, has now not only stopped but also been repelled, and a part of it has even collapsed.

In this situation, what needs to be studied is how the enemy will reorganize their troops in the future, and what new plans will be adopted for operations on the Western Front. During this period, this is our most pressing concern. Can the large Russian army on the Eastern Front defeat the enemy? Can the German-Austrian alliance support the two-front war? Their previous concentration on one front has failed.

On August 28th, when I led the Ninth Army, the headquarters' official report stated, "From Kongmu to Fusiqi...the attack was victorious." The official report on July 10th stated, "French victory confirmed..." I am very pleased that our army's turn from defeat to victory is not unrelated.

The German forces attacking the Ninth Army, hoping to break through the French central front, are as follows:

German Second Army丨丨Tenth Army Corps (also attacking the French Tenth Army Corps), Tenth Reserve Army Corps and Guard Army Corps.

German Third Army丨丨Thirteenth Army Corps (Thirty-Second and Twenty-Third Divisions) and Twelfth Reserve Army Corps (Twenty-Third and Twenty-Fourth Reserve Divisions).

While clearing the remnants of the enemy in the Xie Long area, I received the unfortunate news that my family had been suffering on the front line since August 22nd. This news was brought to me by Sarai, the commander of the Third Army. At that time, I was preoccupied with urgent national affairs and had no time to mourn. However, I felt at the time that if these voluntary sacrifices were not in vain, then the victory that had already been achieved would surely be on the rise.

While in Xie Long, many local dignitaries requested to see me. The first was the governor of Mang County, Xie Polong. I apologized to him for occupying part of the area, and gave him hope that we would only need to occupy it for a short period of time. In fact, the headquarters was stationed there for several months. Following Xie Polong was Xi Tiexi, the teacher of Xie Long. He did not leave his church during the German invasion. He was detailing how he personally requested Prince Saxon during the short period of enemy occupation, so that the town could be exempt from heavy donations. At this time, Senator Bai Qiya and Congressmen Meng Hu and Dr. Beixiang also arrived together. We therefore unanimously congratulated the greatness and strength of our beloved France, whose athletes completely forgot the conflicts of political parties and worked together to repel the enemy.

After October 4th, the fighting on the front line of the Ninth Army turned into a period of stagnation, and it stagnated for a long time. The enemy used its powerful artillery to consolidate its superior position, and built several continuous deep trenches, protected by machine guns, with hidden cannons on both wings. This was not the time to drive out the enemy. On September 26th, the enemy's general offensive also completely failed. Our defense became more and more solid day by day. We don't need to worry about how the enemy will attack. In this situation, there is currently no hope of determining victory or defeat in the Xiangben area.

As for what happened on the remaining defense lines in front, especially on the left wing formed by our army, I only vaguely learned a little from the daily official reports. In this confusing state, I received a notification from the Commander-in-Chief on the afternoon of October 4th, calling me to his headquarters in Romelu. I reported there at around 4 p.m.

General Joffre told me that the goal of the Allied left wing's operations had always been to encircle the German right wing. If this plan could not succeed, our strategy could prevent the enemy from making the same move to encircle our left wing. Based on this goal, he had already transferred General Kosternera's Second Army (headquarters in Bailetayi) to the left of the Sixth Army north of Wo Yisi and Sham. General Mabao's detachment (headquarters in Saint Paul) was being ordered to advance with Arras for the same mission. The detachment had been constantly replenished and often ordered to operate independently. On October 5th, the detachment was formed into the Tenth Army.

Responsible for liaison between the Second and Tenth Armies was General Belucci's volunteer corps (headquarters in Duran).

The British army also requested to be transferred from Ai Yisi to our left wing. This request has been approved. The transfer will be carried out soon. The British army headquarters will be located in Saint Amel. Finally, the Belgian army gathered near Antewerp will sooner or later find a way to cooperate. Because several commanders in this area were a little hesitant and hoped to reach a satisfactory compromise with our Allied forces, the Commander-in-Chief decided to appoint me as the Assistant to the Commander-in-Chief to go to the Northern Front immediately to command and assist the Allied forces in combat.
